[0m[1m	<script type='text/javascript'>\n
[0m[1m	//<![CDATA[\n
[0m[1m	var relatedTitles = new Array();\n
[0m[1m	var relatedTitlesNum = 0;\n
[0m[1m	var relatedUrls = new Array();\n
[0m[1m	function related_results_labels(json) {\n
[0m[1m	for (var i = 0; i < json.feed.entry.length; i++) {\n
[0m[1m	var entry = json.feed.entry[i];\n
[0m[1m	relatedTitles[relatedTitlesNum] = entry.title.$t;\n
[0m[1m	for (var k = 0; k < entry.link.length; k++) {\n
[0m[1m	if (entry.link[k].rel == 'alternate') {\n
[0m[1m	relatedUrls[relatedTitlesNum] = entry.link[k].href;\n
[0m[1m	relatedTitlesNum++;\n
[0m[1m	break;\n
[0m[1m	}\n
[0m[1m	}\n
[0m[1m	}\n
[0m[1m	}\n
[0m[1m	function removeRelatedDuplicates() {\n
[0m[1m	var tmp = new Array(0);\n
[0m[1m	var tmp2 = new Array(0);\n
[0m[1m	for(var i = 0; i < relatedUrls.length; i++) {\n
[0m[1m	if(!contains(tmp, relatedUrls[i])) {\n
[0m[1m	tmp.length += 1;\n
[0m[1m	tmp[tmp.length - 1] = relatedUrls[i];\n
[0m[1m	tmp2.length += 1;\n
[0m[1m	tmp2[tmp2.length - 1] = relatedTitles[i];\n
[0m[1m	}\n
[0m[1m	}\n
[0m[1m	relatedTitles = tmp2;\n
[0m[1m	relatedUrls = tmp;\n
[0m[1m	}\n
[0m[1m	function contains(a, e) {\n
[0m[1m	for(var j = 0; j < a.length; j++) if (a[j]==e) return true;\n
[0m[1m	return false;\n
[0m[1m	}\n
[0m[1m	function printRelatedLabels() {\n
[0m[1m	var r = Math.floor((relatedTitles.length - 1) * Math.random());\n
[0m[1m	var i = 0;\n
[0m[1m	document.write('<ul>');\n
[0m[1m	while (i < relatedTitles.length && i < 20) {\n
[0m[1m	document.write('<li><a href="' + relatedUrls[r] + '">' + relatedTitles[r] + '</a></li>');\n
[0m[1m	if (r < relatedTitles.length - 1) {\n
[0m[1m	r++;\n
[0m[1m	} else {\n
[0m[1m	r = 0;\n
[0m[1m	}\n
[0m[1m	i++;\n
[0m[1m	}\n
[0m[1m	document.write('</ul>');\n
[0m[1m	}\n
[0m[1m	//]]>\n
[0m[1m	</script>\n
[0m[1m	<script type='text/javascript'>\n
[0m[1m	\n
[0m[1m	    var fade = false;\n
[0m[1m	    function showFull(id) {\n
[0m[1m	    var post = document.getElementById(id);\n
[0m[1m	    var spans = post.getElementsByTagName('span');\n
[0m[1m	    for (var i = 0; i < spans.length; i++) {\n
[0m[1m	    if (spans[i].id == "fullpost") {\n
[0m[1m	    if (fade) {\n
[0m[1m	    spans[i].style.background = peekaboo_bgcolor;\n
[0m[1m	    Effect.Appear(spans[i]);\n
[0m[1m	    } else spans[i].style.display = 'inline';\n
[0m[1m	    }\n
[0m[1m	    if (spans[i].id == "showlink")\n
[0m[1m	    spans[i].style.display = 'none';\n
[0m[1m	    if (spans[i].id == "hidelink")\n
[0m[1m	    spans[i].style.display = 'inline';\n
[0m[1m	    }\n
[0m[1m	    }\n
[0m[1m	\n
[0m[1m	\n
[0m[1m	    function hideFull(id) {\n
[0m[1m	    var post = document.getElementById(id);\n
[0m[1m	    var spans = post.getElementsByTagName('span');\n
[0m[1m	    for (var i = 0; i < spans.length; i++) {\n
[0m[1m	    if (spans[i].id == "fullpost") {\n
[0m[1m	    if (fade) {\n
[0m[1m	    spans[i].style.background = peekaboo_bgcolor;\n
[0m[1m	    Effect.Fade(spans[i]);\n
[0m[1m	    } else spans[i].style.display = 'none';\n
[0m[1m	    }\n
[0m[1m	    if (spans[i].id == "showlink")\n
[0m[1m	    spans[i].style.display = 'inline';\n
[0m[1m	    if (spans[i].id == "hidelink")\n
[0m[1m	    spans[i].style.display = 'none';\n
[0m[1m	    }\n
[0m[1m	    post.scrollIntoView(true);\n
[0m[1m	    }\n
[0m[1m	\n
[0m[1m	    function checkFull(id) {\n
[0m[1m	    var post = document.getElementById(id);\n
[0m[1m	    var spans = post.getElementsByTagName('span');\n
[0m[1m	    var found = 0;\n
[0m[1m	    for (var i = 0; i < spans.length; i++) {\n
[0m[1m	    if (spans[i].id == "fullpost") {\n
[0m[1m	    spans[i].style.display = 'none';\n
[0m[1m	    found = 1;\n
[0m[1m	    }\n
[0m[1m	    if ((spans[i].id == "showlink") && (found == 0))\n
[0m[1m	    spans[i].style.display = 'none';\n
[0m[1m	    }\n
[0m[1m	    }\n
[0m[1m	\n
